Lease of Mining Rights and Relationship Between Roads and Mining Areas 50

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry recently explained the lease of mining rights and the relationship between roads and mining areas as follows: Mining rights, except for inheritance, transfer, mortgage, delayed payment disposal, and compulsory execution, shall not be the purpose of rights, as clearly stipulated in Article 14, Paragraph 1 of the Mining Law. If a mining right holder requests to lease the mining right, it violates the provisions of this article and should not be approved. If a mining right holder entrusts others to manage the business on their behalf, and the content of the contract has the nature of leasing or pawning, it can be rejected when reporting. If it has been implemented without reporting, the contract is invalid, but how to punish it should be decided by the court. As for the public roads referred to in Article 22, Paragraph 3 of the Mining Law, they naturally include national, provincial, county, township, and district roads. When opening up the above-mentioned public roads, it is appropriate to find a way to bypass the areas that have been designated as mining areas. (Central News Agency, 14th)

Key Points of the Parcel Tariff Table 56

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications has completed the revision of the parcel tariff table, which will be implemented from the first of next month. Its main points are: 1. The standard of tariffs is determined according to the amount of freight; 2. Parcel tariffs are collected at the originating局, and no additional fees are added at the destination局; 3. Fees are charged per kilogram, which is simple and easy to understand; 4. All parcel tariffs are listed in the parcel tariff table, without exception, and can be found by checking the (Compilation of Post Office Locations); 5. The parcel tariffs for mutual postage between all bureaus in the country are clearly stipulated, without any ambiguity; 6. Business people and others who want to know the parcel postage only need to consult the Compilation of Post Office Locations and the Parcel Tariff Table to know the exact postage to any location in the country. (Special Dispatch, 14th)

Ministry of Foreign Affairs Advises Provinces and Cities Not to Detain Foreign Passports Without Authorization 57

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has advised all provinces and cities that foreign missionaries traveling to the interior often have their passports confiscated by military police because the validity period of the passport itself is not stipulated, which leads to questions from foreigners. This type of situation is especially common for French priests. It should be known that although the right to sign foreign passports is in our hands, the right to stipulate the effective time of the passport belongs to the issuing country, and it is not convenient for us to interfere. In the future, if local authorities encounter foreign travel passports and missionary passports whose visas have expired, they should immediately advise them to apply for a new visa and inform them that the purpose of the visa is to facilitate investigation and achieve the purpose of sufficient protection, except for the locations where they can pass through and reside. There is no restriction on travel and missionary work. If priests are in remote areas and it is inconvenient to go to the county government to request a visa, they should immediately transfer the expired passport to the county government for a new visa at the nearest public security bureau and return the passport to the individual as quickly as possible. All passports that have not been visaed should be visaed immediately. If a visa has already expired, it should be renewed immediately. The original passport should not be detained, which will cause misunderstandings among foreigners. (Special Dispatch, 14th)

Wuhan Dikes Continue to Collapse; Hanyang County Completely Flooded; Corpses Cover the River; Wuchang Plans to Build Second Line of Defense; Zhang Gong Dike in Critical Condition; General Mobilization for Rescue 78

A dispatch from Hankou: In recent days, the Xiang River has risen sharply, and the water from Dongting Lake has overflowed, converging at Hankou. The water level has risen to 51 feet 4 inches, and all dikes in Wuhan are in a state of emergency. On the 12th, the Changfeng South Embankment in Hankou collapsed, causing a vast inundation of hundreds of miles, stretching from Duoluokou, passing through Xiaojiadi, Luojiadun, Hanjiadun, Jiangjiadun, Xinjiadi, Zhoujiadun, to the factories of the British American Tobacco Company, and the villages along the Hankou-Yichang Road. This embankment and the Changfeng North Embankment are both protections for the Zhang Gong Dike, which in turn protects the entire city of Hankou. On the 11th, the North Embankment collapsed, and the Zhang Gong Dike was already in danger. The collapse of the South Embankment further aggravated the situation, so the Zhang Gong Dike, known for its solidity, is in danger of collapsing at any time. Mayor Wu Guozhen and Police Chief Chen Xizeng have been inspecting and directing the rescue efforts at the dike for several days, but it is still difficult to reverse the critical situation. On the 13th, a section of the dike in Huangjia Xiaowan collapsed once, and the foot of the dike in the Jinkou section between Qiaokou and Gusaoshu collapsed by more than two zhang. Dan Shui Chi, Fenjin Lu, and Chen Jia Ji experienced severe seepage. The cement dikes along the Yangtze River from the Jianghan Customs Wharf, passing through Special District 3, Special District 2, the French Concession, Special District 1, to the Japanese Concession, all leaked water. If the river rises by another foot or so, it could overflow the dikes and flood the entire city. Pacification Commissioner He Chengjun and Provincial Chairman Zhang Qun believe that the safety of Hankou depends on the Zhang Gong Dike, so they paid special attention to the rescue efforts at the dike. On the 13th, He Chengjun and Zhang Qun both supervised the work at the dike, and garrison troops and police also participated. However, it was difficult to conscript civilian laborers. In order to facilitate the rescue work, Zhang Qun specially authorized Garrison Commander Su Peng to take full responsibility for flood control in Hankou. The Municipal Government, the Public Security Bureau, and the Jianghan Engineering Bureau are all under his command. If necessary, he can forcibly conscript labor and materials. Anyone who disobeys orders, obstructs work, or neglects their duties will be immediately sent to the Garrison Headquarters for strict punishment according to military law. After taking office, Ye took up his post at the dike. When Huangjia Xiaowan was in danger, he supervised the rescue work and only turned the situation around by the evening. On the 13th, all sectors of the Party, government, military, and police were mobilized for the rescue work, so the results were quite good. However, while Hankou was temporarily preserved, Hanyang suffered even greater disasters. The Sanyanqiao Dike on the opposite bank of Duoluokou was breached by the Xiang River. All 72 wards of the county were flooded, and many people and animals drowned. Corpses covered the river, a truly tragic sight. In Wuchang, the Wufeng Dike is probably beyond repair, and the dikes along the river are also in critical condition. Personnel from the Provincial Flood Control Committee have been working hard for days, and their work is gradually becoming lax. Liu Shoupeng, Director of the Department of Construction, Cai Mengjian, Chief of the Public Security Bureau, and Zheng Shisheng, the county magistrate, are supervising the rescue efforts and have already designated a second line of defense. If the dikes unfortunately collapse, they will retreat to the new defense. In the counties upstream and downstream, dikes and embankments continue to collapse. Reports of disasters have reached 36 counties and cities, and communication has been cut off in several places. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek yesterday again telegraphed the authorities in Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Anhui, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang to strictly protect the dikes and instruct each county magistrate in the dike counties to inspect the dikes, examine the dangers, and immediately supervise the people to work in case of danger. All materials for flood control should be strictly prohibited from being hoarded by shops to avoid delaying the work. (13th)

Yellow River Flood in Shandong Still Extremely Serious; Breaches Occur Successively in the People's Embankments of Fan County and Shou Zhang; Heavy Rain Throughout the Province; Water Level of Various Rivers Increases 79

A dispatch from Jinan: The Yellow River breach in Juancheng, Shandong, has affected Yuncheng, Heze, Dongping, Juye, and Jiaxiang counties. After a severe drought, the people have suffered this great calamity, which is extremely pitiful. Moreover, from the evening of the 12th to the afternoon of the 13th, there was continuous heavy rain throughout the province. The people's embankments on the south bank of Shou Zhang and the north bank of Fan County have successively collapsed, and the disaster area is expanding daily. The Dongzhuang (Juancheng) breach has been widened by rainwater erosion, and the two breaches have been washed into one large breach, more than 200 zhang wide. The rivers throughout the province have risen, a serious situation not seen in years. In addition to repeatedly telegraphing the central government to request funds for damming the breach and providing disaster relief and requesting punishment for himself, Han Fuju again telegraphed Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman Lin Sen, President Wang Jingwei, Song Ziwen, Chairman of the National Economic Council, and Li Yizhi, Chairman of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Committee in Kaifeng, on the 13th to report the expansion of the breach and the flood situation. At the same time, he specially appointed Zhang Honglie, Director of the Department of Construction, to represent him in Beijing to meet with important figures in the central government, explain everything in detail, and discuss the allocation of funds for damming the breach and providing disaster relief. He will also represent him at the National Water Conservancy Conference. Zhang Honglie took the train to Shanghai on the morning of the 14th, carrying the handwritten notes that Han Fuju intended to present to the central government.

Breaches Merge into Large Breaches

According to reports from the magistrates of Juan, He, Fan, and Yun counties and Wang Shaochang, the commissioner of the Shandong Experimental Zone, the official dike at Dongzhuang collapsed. From the evening of the 12th, due to heavy rain and rising water, the breaches have been eroded and merged into one large breach, more than 200 zhang wide. The Yellow River rushes out wildly, accounting for 70% of the main river's flow. The breach exceeding the Jiangsu Dam and irrigating Yuncheng County is currently 30 li away from the county seat of Yuncheng. The county is rushing to repair the city protection dike day and night. The breach irrigating Heze is currently about 3 li away from the city. The city protection dike that the county was rushing to build has been destroyed by the strong current. The county town is even more critical. The current is flowing eastward and merging with Wang Lan Lake in Yun County. There is a possibility that the flood will flow into the Nanyang River. Now Jinxiang, Jiaxiang, Yutai and other counties along the lake are rushing to repair dikes near the Nanyang Lake to prevent inundation. At the same time, Wang Shaochang, the head of the Luxi County Political Construction Experiment, specially telegraphed the counties near Lu in northern Jiangsu to quickly build dikes near the Nanyang Lake to prevent inundation. Sun Zerang, the head of the Heze Experimental County, went to Dongzhuang in person on the 13th to meet with Zhang Lianjia, director of the River Affairs Bureau, to discuss the damming of the breach and other matters, and to raise 3 million catties of straw for use in damming the breach. Wang Shaochang believed that the breaches are getting larger and should be dammed as soon as possible, so he submitted a request to the provincial government to order students from rural agricultural schools to bring a cart of straw each to Dongzhuang to dam the breach. Han Fuju has approved this and is proceeding with it. While various parties were building the breach and preparing to prevent inundation, the people's embankments in the two counties of Shou Zhang and Fan County upstream successively collapsed. On the evening of the 12th, when there was heavy rain, the Huanghua Guan on the south bank of Zhang County suddenly collapsed, and the flood flowed back. On the morning of the 13th, the backflow had passed Wang Lou and the Shu Xilou in Yuncheng County and reached Liukou. Fan County and Juancheng are all a vast expanse of water. According to a report from Fan County, the Bai Zhuang people's embankment on the north bank collapsed on the evening of the 12th, and the floodwaters have reached Sunkou Town. Residents along the river are adding small embankments along the Yellow River dike. All the houses and fields within the embankments are flooded and have become a swamp. The scorpion bay in Poutai County and the Zhao Jia Dam in Bin County have been partially submerged, and the situation is extremely dangerous. Urgent telegrams have been sent from all sections. Now the water level in the middle and lower reaches has slightly decreased. The water level in Luokou in the middle reaches is 30.66 meters. It is rumored that the Heigang breach in Henan Province also occurred on the evening of the 12th, with two breaches. One flows southeast directly to Kaifeng, and the other irrigates Dongming County in Hebei Province and heads towards Luxi. If this news is confirmed, then Cao's counties will inevitably be flooded again. The Provincial River Affairs Bureau believes that the Yellow River situation is so serious that it is truly at a critical juncture. It immediately dispatched flood control personnel on the 13th to various dangerous sections along the river, carrying hemp ropes, burlap sacks, and other materials to prepare for emergency rescue at any time. It is said that they have all arrived at their posts.

Shidian in Lijin Suddenly in Danger

In Lijin, downstream on the Yellow River, the Luang Zikou was used to carry out immigration and reclamation. Zhao Mingyuan, the commander of the First Route Militia, supervised the soldiers and civilians to build a cofferdam, and the Dachang was repaired for dozens of miles. However, the section from Luan Jingzikou and above has not yet been completely repaired. On the 12th, the Yellow River suddenly rose sharply, and the torrent scoured the Shidian in the territory of Lijin County above the Luang Jingzikou. The river water overflowed, and is currently being rescued. However, the details have not been reported to the authorities. The people in the plantation area are all very scared. Zhao Mingyuan came to Jinan a few days ago to report on the immigration situation. Now he heard the news and immediately rushed back to Lijin.

Heavy Rain in the Midst of the Flood

The flood is already extremely serious, but on the afternoon of the 12th, there was a torrential downpour all over the province, from the northeast to the southeast. Not only did the Yellow River rise, and the flood victims were in danger, but also the rivers throughout the province were rising, and the reports of collapsed dikes and embankments were flying like snowflakes. The provincial government has telegraphed the county chiefs along the river to step up their efforts to protect them, so as to avoid accidents. Many of the province's power lines and long-distance communication lines have been damaged and are being repaired. From the 12th to the morning of the 13th, Jinan received 46.8 mm of rainfall. It rained again in the afternoon, although it stopped soon afterwards. Up to the evening, it was still not sunny. The heavy rain on the 12th was the heaviest in eastern Shandong, so it washed away a section of the roadbed east of the Zhangdian station on the Jiaoji Railway. The roadbed east of Zhangdian was very high, and it took a lot of effort for freight cars to go uphill. Therefore, when the Zhangdian marshalling yard was built a few days ago, the roadbed was lowered. Unexpectedly, the heavy rain on the night of the 12th turned into a river, which washed away a section of the newly built roadbed, causing the tracks to hang in the air and preventing vehicles from passing. On the same night, one westbound train stopped in Qingzhou, and two eastbound trains stopped in Zhangdian, and traffic was interrupted. On the morning of the 13th, the Jiaoji Railway Bureau sent an engineer with workers and materials to repair it, and the work was completed at about 11:00 a.m. The trains ran as usual. The first train arrived in Jinan at a little after 1:00 p.m., a delay of six hours. (13th)

Chairman Chiang's Speech on the Responsibility of Youth (Continued) - Attending the Expanded Memorial Week in Chengdu - 80

Therefore, everyone should cultivate this habit of labor and develop this spirit of service. In the future, everyone should do at least one thing a day that benefits others to create happiness for society. Extending this further, we can do the great cause of governing the country and bringing peace to the world.

Fourth, we must recognize our position and responsibility in the family. You must understand that the position and responsibility of children in the family and your position and responsibility in the country, although different in scope, are the same in principle. You must be a loyal citizen in the country and a virtuous and filial son in the family. Be filial to your parents, respect your elder brothers, and love your younger siblings. You must also develop the virtues of filial piety, friendship, harmony, and care to foster good relations with neighbors and extend them to clan members, villages, relatives, and friends. Love each other, encourage each other in morality, share weal and woe, help each other, and support each other in illness. As for parents and elder brothers in the family, they should also be responsible for teaching their children well, making them know the principles of being a good person. They should also supervise them to learn to work hard, and not let them be lazy and become parasites who harm the family and the country. I can tell you that when I was young, my family was considered well-off, but I still had to wash clothes, sweep the floor, cook, and do other kinds of household chores every day. My mother also supervised me to do this every day, because this is the most basic and important principle of being a good person. We must cultivate this spirit and habit of labor and service in the family from childhood. When we grow up, we can be a healthy citizen. Now there are many elementary school students who not only cannot serve and be filial to their elders in the family, but often have their parents serve them everything, such as serving meals and washing clothes. This is not the principle of being a child. If they are unwilling to do things for themselves and their families, how can they serve society and the country in the future? In general, people who are parents do not teach their children to work hard, which makes their children's bodies become weaker and their spirits become more depressed. This kind of complacency is harmful, and it is not the principle of being a parent. Therefore, you, the general young students, must first respect your parents and elders, respect your elder brothers and love your younger brothers, and harmonize with your neighbors in the family. Secondly, you should labor. All kinds of things, such as fetching water, sweeping, washing, cooking, and gardening, must be done by ourselves to serve the whole family. From this, we can cultivate noble personality, forge a strong physique, and lay the foundation for a healthy citizen.

Fifth, we must recognize our position and responsibility in schools and groups. Schools are also a kind of group. Now the military training groups you are in are also schools. In school, you should of course expect to be excellent students. Excellent young students are the most healthy fighters who protect the country and defend the people. Therefore, all schools, whether teachers or students, must strive to be a healthy fighter. To be a healthy fighter, we must pay special attention to the cultivation of personality, the deepening of knowledge, and the training of the body. But in addition to this, we must also have a spirit of love for the group and the habits of group life. First, we must be able to be affectionate and sincere, and unite as one. At ordinary times, we must love our classmates, and not argue with each other or only seek convenience for ourselves and harm the interests of the group and others. We must always take care of everyone's interests. If friends have difficulties, we must help them. If friends are sick, we must help them. We should love each other like hands and feet, and share each other's hardships and joys. We must unite with sincerity and cooperate. Only in this way can we share difficulties and live and die together, give full play to common and consistent strength, and achieve the common and consistent goal of saving the country. Everyone should cultivate this spirit while they are in school. This spirit is the real power of saving our country. Second, we must obey our leaders. A group must have a leader. The principal of the school, the directors of the departments, the teachers in charge of each class, the leaders of the Boy Scouts or military training groups, the platoon leaders, and the squad leaders are your leaders in the group. You are their subordinates. Subordinates must obey their leaders. The leaders are the people who lead the group. All legal orders of the leaders are the supreme will of the group and the norm for the actions of the members. If a group does not have a leader, it is like a ship without a rudder and cannot become a group. Therefore, you must take obedience to your leaders as your duty and abide by their orders in order to exert the power of the group. Third, we must strictly abide by the rules. Rules are a necessary condition for maintaining group life and an essential element for saving and building the country. If a group does not have rules, it will not have system and cannot be maintained. With rules, there will be common and consistent actions and a common and consistent spirit and power will be generated. The school rules of your school, the rules or military discipline of the Boy Scouts or military training groups, and the laws and regulations of governments at all levels are all rules. The most important cultivation of modern citizens is to pay attention to order and abide by discipline. Whether in class or out of class, or marching and walking, or even in all life and actions, we must abide by certain order and discipline. We now want to save the country and restore the national freedom and equality, which is that everyone abides by discipline and everyone works hard on a common and consistent track. Therefore, all principals and teachers must pay special attention to the spirit of group order and discipline and not allow anyone to disrupt order or break discipline. If the principal and teachers do not fulfill this responsibility, they will harm the students, the school, and the country. The last point is to cultivate the spirit of courage, decisiveness, and adventure through the practice and encouragement of group life. The head should enable each member and the entire group to be full of vigor at all times. Everyone should strive to be enterprising, see righteousness and act courageously, and be able to make wise decisions when things happen. Once a decision is made, no difficulty or danger is enough to move us. As long as it is beneficial to the group, to society, and to the country and the nation, we will not hesitate to sacrifice and take risks to achieve our goals. This spirit and habit of sacrificing oneself for the group and fighting bravely is the true spirit of the revival of the nation (to be continued).

Worker at Shenxin Cotton Mill Dies of Heatstroke

Since the 10th of this month, the weather in this county has turned hot, with the Fahrenheit thermometer rising to over 90 degrees. The heat has been even more intense since the day before yesterday. Yesterday (the 14th), the indoor temperature rose to 98 degrees, and under the scorching sun, it was over 110 degrees. Therefore, ordinary laborers are suffering greatly working under the blazing sun, and many are suffering from heatstroke. Yesterday morning, around 1:00 AM, a worker named Xiao Heshang (over 30 years old) in the machine room of the Shenxin Third Cotton Mill in this county suddenly fainted and fell to the ground due to the stifling heat and died shortly after. It is indeed a tragic event.

Changzhou 83

Night Train Engine Caught Carrying Smuggled Soil

According to a tip-off received by the Su-Dan First Section of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Police, a large quantity of smuggled soil was being transported to Changzhou on the night of the 12th. Section Chief Jiang dispatched Inspector Yao with nine policemen, disguised as laborers, to lie in the grass east of the station in Waiyangqi at around 1:00 AM on the 13th. At around 3:00 AM, the No. 6 night express train from Shanghai to Beijing passed by. They saw a green light shining from the engine near the railway. As they approached the light, burlap sacks were thrown down, and several people came forward to pick them up. The police rushed out of the grass, apprehended the people and the sacks, and brought them to the station to be weighed by the stationmaster, along with witnesses. There were seven sacks of smuggled soil, weighing 22 kilograms, equivalent to about 500 taels in the market. The stationmaster stamped them with the fire stamp. Inspector Yao and others took the witnesses back to the police station for preliminary interrogation. The bag recipients were identified as Gao Liuchun, the main offender, and Zhang San, both residents near the station. After interrogation, the Shanghai Railway Police Department was notified for further investigation. The driver of the No. 6 night train, Liu Da, and two stokers were arrested in Beijing by the Beijing station at the request of the Changzhou station due to work schedule constraints. The Changzhou station police section has sent officers to Beijing to escort them back to Changzhou for interrogation.

Jiaxing 89

Investigation Reveals Dispute Involving Nine Raw Opium Dealers

At approximately 10:00 AM on the 13th, a passenger named Zhou Zhonghua (27 years old, from Jiangwan, Shanghai), carrying a leather suitcase, walked out of the main entrance of the station as the Shanghai-bound morning express train arrived in He. He immediately hired a rickshaw. Chen Bingkui, a marine police detective, noticed him and suspected his movements. He stepped forward and ordered him to stop, which led to a dispute. The railway police officer and patrol leader stepped forward to detain Zhou Zhonghua and took him back to the station. The stationmaster was notified to open the suitcase, which revealed six large packages of raw opium (totaling 24 jin in market weight). The marine police detective requested to take the opium dealer away, but the railway police argued that the area where the arrest was made was within the jurisdiction of the Jiaxing station, and the case should be handed over to their superiors. Subsequently, personnel from the 5th Marine Police Detachment arrived at the station to escort him, but the patrol leader refused, almost leading to a misunderstanding. Land police also arrived to request, but to no effect. It was not until approximately 5:00 PM that Liao Mianqing, the chief of the Jia閘 sub-section, arrived in He by car. After consulting with the marine police personnel, the marine police detachment prepared an official letter to take the opium dealer and the opium away. However, according to Zhou Zhonghua, he is a tailor and was invited by a friend named Zhao to visit He. The suitcase belonged to Zhao and was entrusted to him to carry, but he did not know it contained opium. He claimed that Zhao had left on the train when the marine police detective questioned him.

Linpu Town in Xiaoshan, located on the border of Shaoxing and Xiaoshan counties, is the most prosperous commercial town. Its commerce has always been flourishing. Moreover, Wanlong South Goods Store has also recently closed. It is said that the losses are quite substantial. The decline of commerce in the town is evident.

Local News

Baoshan County Magistrate Long Inspects Seawall Construction the Day Before Yesterday, Strictly Orders Seawall Guards to Pay Attention at All Times 92

The Baoshan County seawall is a barrier for the counties of Shanghai, Taicang, Jiading, and Baoshan, and a crucial point on the river and sea. At a time when the Yangtze River flood is severe, the safety of the seawall construction there is of great concern to society. A reporter from Dabai News Agency went to Baoshan County to inquire about the details and recorded them as follows:

Seawall Construction Solidly Repaired Last Year

In the summer and autumn floods of the year before last, the Baoshan seawall was in danger in many places due to frequent wind and rain. Although it was repaired at that time, due to insufficient funds, the project was inevitably not solid. Last year, the Jiangsu Provincial authorities, recognizing the importance of the Baoshan seawall, allocated funds from the Taicang, Jiading, and Baoshan Relief Institute to greatly repair it. The entire seawall project was thus doubled in solidity. Usually, the county government strictly supervises the Seawall Engineering Office to pay attention at all times.

This Year's Plum Rains Caused Minor Damage

During this year's plum rains last month, when the water rose, the waves at the Sanjia Water area outside Wusongkou were particularly large. The seawall was greatly impacted by the torrents. Fortunately, the seawall was built solidly and did not suffer much impact. Only the lower-lying sections of the seawall suffered minor damage. After the Seawall Engineering Office repaired it, there was no major concern.

County Magistrate Inspects Entire Seawall Construction Project

Baoshan County Magistrate Long Tiyao, concerned that the Baoshan seawall might be endangered by the rising waters of the Yangtze River due to the severe Yangtze River flood, went to Shidong, Xuejiatan, Longwang Temple, Wuhedun, and other sections on the day before yesterday with Secretary Wang Rongsan, Third Section Chief Qi Yunzhong, and seawall guards to conduct a detailed inspection. He strictly ordered the seawall guards to supervise and urge the Seawall Engineering Office to pay attention to repairs at all times to avoid danger.

Xu Shiying Departs for the Yangtze River This Morning to Inspect Disaster Areas in Various Provinces; Disaster Relief Funds of Two Million Yuan to Be Allocated Monthly; Custodial Committee to Be Established This Month 93

Xu Shiying, Chairman of the National Government Relief Committee, is extremely concerned about the flood disaster. He went to Nanjing a few days ago to discuss disaster relief funds with government officials. It is reported that the disaster relief fund of two million yuan for this year will be allocated by the Ministry of Finance from the national treasury at more than 160,000 yuan per month, to be fully disbursed in twelve months for reserve use. This time, the funds will be diverted for immediate use due to the urgent need for disaster relief. The establishment of the custodial committee is expected to be completed within this month. There will be a total of seven committee members. The Ministries of Finance and Interior, and the Relief Committee will each send one member as ex-officio members. The remaining four members will be appointed by the government from fair and important officials. After the committee is established, two standing committee members will be appointed, with one chairman serving as the standing committee member, to be in charge of affairs. The committee's affairs will be handled concurrently by the Relief Committee, without incurring additional expenses, in order to save public funds. Mr. Xu is going to inspect the disaster areas in various provinces along the Yangtze River. He boarded the Jiang'an ship last night and set sail upstream this morning. He will rush back to Nanjing at the end of the month to attend the custodial committee meeting. It is said that at the beginning of the next month, he will need to go to Huangshan to inspect via an intermediate route.

Chu Minyi Discusses Director Wang's Illness; Inflammation of Gallbladder Due to Hot Weather Has Not Subsided; Requires Four or Five Weeks of Recuperation to Recover 97

Chen Shaokuan, Minister of the Navy, accompanied by Yang Qingzhen, Director of the General Affairs Department of the Ministry, Zheng Zixi, Director of the Ordnance Bureau, and telegraph operators and secretaries, left Shanghai for Fujian on the Hai Chou warship at 10:00 AM yesterday. The heads of various naval agencies in Shanghai, including Ma Deji, Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard, Liu Defu, Director of the Survey Bureau, Wu Zhennan, Director of the Coastal Patrol, Gao Xianzhong, Director of the Pilot Training Institute, Lin Yuanquan, Director of the Ordnance Department, Ye Baoqi, Commander of the Guard Battalion, Staff Officer Liu of the Training Fleet Headquarters, Adjutant Chen, and Zeng Yijing, Director of the Aircraft Office, all went to the Hai Chou warship at 8:00 AM to see him off. Mr. Chen will first go to Fuzhou and then to Xiamen. He is expected to return to Shanghai by the end of this month. During Mr. Chen's absence from Nanjing, the routine affairs of the Ministry will be handled by Chen Jiliang, the Vice Minister of Political Affairs.

Chen Ce Telegraphs Shanghai; Two Warships Will Arrive in Shanghai in the Coming Days; Currently Still Docked in Zhenhai, Not Yet Set Sail 100

According to the Central News Agency, Chen Ce, Director of the Military Affairs Department of the Military Affairs Commission, led the Haiqi and Haishen warships out of Hong Kong on the 9th and arrived in Zhenhai on the 12th to dock. Mr. Chen telegraphed his friends in Shanghai yesterday, saying, "I have arrived safely in Zhenhai and will come to Shanghai and then to Nanjing in the coming days." The telegram was sent yesterday morning, which proves that the two warships were still in Zhenhai yesterday and had not yet set sail north. According to Mr. Chen's friends, the two warships are currently in good condition, and the rumor that the machinery is damaged is not true. Now that the two warships have arrived in Zhenhai, they have effectively returned north, so there is no need to rush to Nanjing.

Yesterday was the 146th anniversary of French National Day, which coincided with Sunday. All French government, commercial, and organizational bodies in the city were closed. French warships moored on the Bund of the French Concession shone searchlights in the evening.

The Crew of the Maoli No. 2 Arrive in Shanghai, Report Six Drowned After Ship Sank, Including Two Passengers, Three Vendors, One Unidentified 102

After the new Maoli No. 2 steamship of the Maoli Shipping Bureau sank near the Dinghai wharf during its maiden voyage, the crew, including A Yin, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning. According to reports, a total of six people drowned. Salvage operations for the ship and cargo are underway, and post-disaster arrangements are being made. The details are as follows:

Crew Arrive in Shanghai

Twenty-two crew members of the Maoli No. 2 steamship, including Jiang A Yin and stewards, arrived in Shanghai at 7 a.m. yesterday morning aboard the Danshan steamship of the Lian'an Shipping Bureau. They immediately reported the sinking to Hong Baoshun, the owner of the bureau. The ship was carrying approximately 450 passengers when it sailed from Shanghai to Taiwan on the evening of the 11th, including over 200 pilgrims heading to Putuo, about 100 heading to Dinghai, and the remaining 100 or so heading to Shipu, Haimen, Huangyan, and other places. It anchored in the Da Ji ocean area due to fog. Upon arriving at Putuo, all the pilgrims disembarked. At 4 p.m. on the 12th, it arrived in Dinghai and docked at the wharf.

Account of the Sinking

The ship was scheduled to stay at the Dinghai wharf for three hours, allowing people from all walks of life to visit and observe, as well as to load and unload cargo. By around 6 p.m., seven or eight out of ten passengers had disembarked to sightsee and had not returned. About three or four hundred people boarded the ship to look around. At the same time, firecrackers were lit on the wharf, and visitors on the ship flocked to the deck on the wharf side to watch the welcoming scene. This caused the ship to list, and water entered through the stern doors. Passengers and visitors on board scrambled to escape to the shore. The captain and first mate were unable to stop them, leading to the ship sinking in about fifty minutes.

Recovered Bodies

The Dinghai branch immediately dispatched eight divers to investigate and recovered six bodies from the main cabin: three boys around fourteen or fifteen years old, an elderly woman, an elderly man, and a middle-aged man. The elderly woman and man were passengers in the main cabin and were the parents-in-law of A Liu from Taizhou. The three boys were likely vendors who boarded the ship temporarily. Whether the middle-aged man was a passenger or a visitor could not be confirmed at the time. When the ship sank, forty or fifty small boats gathered to provide rescue.

Handling the Aftermath

The Dinghai branch manager, Zhu, along with the ship owner, Xu Yousheng, and compradore, Shi Cantang, made arrangements for the aftermath. They provided travel expenses of one silver dollar each to all 145 stewards on the ship, ordering them to return to their hometowns first. Except for 20 stewards who took the Zhoushan steamship back to Shanghai, the rest took the Dahua steamship back to Haimen. The six recovered bodies have been placed in the local guild hall, awaiting identification by their families. The bureau has decided to provide compensation to the victims.

Salvaging the Ship and Cargo

The Shanghai head office commissioned the China Salvage Company to send 32 people, including engineers, laborers, and divers, accompanied by Zhou Bolun of the bureau, to rush to the scene aboard the Lian'an Gongji Daxing steamship to begin salvage work. They arrived at 7 a.m. yesterday morning and began salvage operations, deciding to first retrieve the cargo and then salvage the steamship. It is said that when the tide is low, four or five feet of the deck is visible above the water, and when the tide is high, two feet are visible. The smokestack and mast are all above the water, and since the location is next to the wharf, salvage should be easy.

Insurance Company Inspection

The China Ship Insurance Association insured the ship for 90,000 national currency in accident insurance. After the sinking, they immediately sent Li Guojie on the Daxing steamship the night before last to inspect the scene. It was found that the ship hull was purchased from the American company Fulai Foreign Firm. After arriving in Shanghai from Ceylon, it was built by the Sino-French Qiuxin Shipyard. All equipment was very complete, making it the best on the Shanghai-Taiwan route. The bottom steel plates are eight-tenths of an inch thick, and the side steel plates are five-tenths of an inch thick. It has only been in operation for twenty-seven years and is very sturdy. It took three months to complete the work, totaling about 150,000 to 160,000 national currency.

Shipping Bureau Announcement

The Maoli head office announced yesterday: "Respectfully informing everyone, our Maoli No. 2 steamship departed from Shanghai on the 11th of this month at 6 p.m. for Putuo, Dinghai, Shipu, Haimen, Huangyan, and other places. It docked at Putuo first and arrived safely in Dinghai at 4 p.m. on the 12th. Around 7 p.m., it was about to depart for Shipu. As the new ship was arriving at the port for the first time, local people held a welcoming ceremony, setting off firecrackers. Passengers came out of the cabins to participate, all leaning to one side, causing the ship to tilt, and water rushed in through the stern doors. It could not be rescued and sank. It is now reported that about six feet is visible above the water at high tide. Fortunately, all passengers and crew are safe. The cargo has been entrusted to the China Salvage Company for salvage, and personnel have been sent to comfort the passengers. A separate report has been submitted to the relevant authorities for protection. Fearing that the outside world does not know the truth, this announcement is made in the newspaper."

Hong's Remarks

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency interviewed Hong Baoshun, the owner of the bureau, at his private residence yesterday morning. According to him, the Maoli No. 2 steamship unfortunately sank next to the Dinghai wharf. Measures have been taken to salvage it and handle the aftermath. It has now been confirmed that the drowned were six vendors. Rumors of it hitting a reef at Laoshu Mountain, damaging the side of the ship, and more than one hundred people drowning are all untrue. Because the accident occurred next to the wharf, and it took fifty minutes to sink, and the mooring ropes were not untied, it was easy to escape. Many small boats nearby provided rescue after the accident, so there is no reason for more than one hundred people to have drowned. He also denied that the Dinghai branch was vandalized by passengers. He also stated that in the news reported by various newspapers about the sinking of his company's Maoli new steamship in Dinghai, the phrase "send divers to Dinghai to salvage ship and cargo" in the telegram reported by compradore Shi Cantang was mistakenly written as "salvage crew." Although it is only one word different, the discrepancy is very large. Please correct it on our behalf.

Rescued Passengers

The Datong News Agency reports that the passengers of the ship have been taken in by local public and private institutions at the Bamin Guild Hall, provided with food, and temporarily maintained. The number of people is 341 in total. The Ministry of Finance Opens the Sichuan-Gansu Unified Tax, Goods to be Taxed in Shanghai First 106

The Ministry of Finance only sets up inspection or management agencies in Sichuan and Gansu, according to Dagong News Agency. In order to rectify tax revenue, the Ministry of Finance instructed the Tax Department to consult with Guan Yuji, the financial commissioner stationed in Sichuan, and the Sichuan Provincial Finance Department to investigate the detailed import and export figures for cotton yarn, cement, matches, etc., and the actual tax revenue compared to the past, in order to implement a unified tax. Now that the 30 million yuan to reorganize Sichuan's financial bonds has been passed by the Legislative Yuan and will be issued on August 1, its funds are guaranteed by the Sichuan unified tax and stamp and tobacco tax revenue. Therefore, the opening of the Sichuan provincial unified tax cannot be delayed. It is now learned that the Ministry of Finance has prepared the measures for opening the Sichuan provincial unified tax, and has also agreed with the Chairman of Gansu Province, Zhu Shaoliang, to open the Gansu Province cigarette unified tax. Both will be officially announced by the Ministry of Finance. According to sources in the Tax Department yesterday, the method for levying the unified tax in Sichuan and Gansu provinces is to first levy taxes on cigarettes sold to Sichuan and Gansu in Shanghai in accordance with the law, and only set up an inspection or management agency in Sichuan and Gansu to prevent smuggling and leakage.

After the Ministry of Finance Postponed the Transaction Tax, Agents from Five Exchanges Sent a Letter of Thanks to Minister Kong, Held the Fifth Current Affairs Meeting Yesterday, Expressing Gratitude for Minister Kong's Consideration of the Difficulties of Business 107

The United Association of Brokers' Associations of the five exchanges in this city decided to send a letter of thanks after Minister Kong showed consideration for the difficulties of business and approved the postponement of the transaction tax. A reporter from the Industry News Agency investigated and recorded the details as follows:

Yesterday's Meeting

The association held its fifth standing committee meeting at Six Horses Road Yizhixiang Western Restaurant at 6 p.m. yesterday. Those present included Bian Futang, Wu Xunqing, Kuang Jian, and Zhang Bojin from the Cotton Yarn Association; Zhan Liansheng, Zhang Zhusun, Gao Qiumei, and Wang Jiafu from the Gold Association; Zhang Weiyun, Zhu Jiansheng, and Xia Rongchang from the Flour Association; He Peiyuan and Qiu Lianggui from the Securities Association; and Xue Chengzhang and Xu Jianqi from the Grain Association, totaling more than ten people. Bian Futang chaired the meeting, and Shao Xingru recorded the minutes. After the usual formalities, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that the five exchanges paid transaction tax to the Ministry of Finance, originally scheduled to be levied on July 1. Later, due to the economic downturn and business difficulties, merchants repeatedly requested postponement. Minister Kong showed consideration for the difficulties of business and approved the postponement, for which the merchants are extremely grateful and should immediately send a letter of thanks. Discussion then began. (1) A motion to send a letter of thanks to Minister Kong for approving the postponement of the transaction tax was passed. (The letter of thanks is detailed below.) (2) A motion proposed by the members of the Gold Association to ban illegal institutions outside the industry from accepting entrusted transactions of gold, cotton yarn, and other goods futures was resolved to request the competent authorities to strictly prohibit them in order to maintain business. (3) Other routine cases were omitted. After the meeting, dinner was served and the meeting adjourned around 9 p.m.

Letter of Thanks to Minister Kong

Humble respects to Minister Kong, the Association and others respectfully submit that, as the government promulgated the transaction tax regulations, it came at a time when the national economy was contracting and industry and commerce were on the verge of danger. Merchants were willing to serve the country but lacked the ability to help the times. Therefore, they dared to repeatedly request your Ministry to consider the difficulties of the times and grant a postponement. The matter was presumptuous, but the situation was unavoidable. Your insight into the difficulties of business and your approval of the request, as indicated in the approved instructions, have been praised throughout the country. Your concern for commerce and your rescue of the people from fire and water have not only allowed the merchants of this association to maintain their business, but the entire industry and commerce have benefited. The gratitude for your kindness is deeply engraved. We respectfully send this humble letter to express our gratitude and respectfully ask for your perusal. The Cotton Yarn Brokers Association, Bian Futang; The Gold Brokers Association, Zhan Liansheng; The Flour Brokers Association, Zhang Weiru; The Grain Brokers Association, Xue Chengzhang; The Securities Brokers Association, He Peiyuan, pay their respects.

The Dispute at the Guangxin Dye Factory, Mediated and Resolved by the City Federation of Trade Unions, Jin Tingsun Donates Funds for Workers' Expenses 109

Dagong News Agency reports that the Guangxin Shengji Dye Factory on Minsheng Road in Zhabei was founded by Ningbo merchants Chen Yuanfu and others and employs more than 100 workers. Recently, due to the economic downturn and intense competition in the industry, the factory was forced to cancel the one-yuan monthly wage for dyeing apprentices, which aroused dissatisfaction among all 40 dyeing workers, who demanded that the factory revoke the order. The factory did not approve. The workers unanimously resigned on their own initiative. The factory paid wages and commissions, but the workers also requested the payment of annual bonuses. The factory stated that the workers were subcontractors and had no bonuses according to the regulations, so it did not approve the request, resulting in a dispute that could not be resolved. The workers petitioned the City Federation of Trade Unions for assistance. Standing Committee Member Shao Lubai, together with factory director Zhu Meixian, conducted mediation. As a result, the workers gave up their demand for bonuses. However, Shao, considering the workers' difficulties, asked Jin Tingsun to donate travel expenses of 14 silver dollars per person, totaling 672 silver dollars, all of which were handed over to the Dyeing Industry Union's Yangse Office for distribution to the workers. The case has been declared successfully resolved.

Ningbo Industrial Bank, The First Voice of Resumption Movement, The Ningbo Industrial Bank Resumption Movement Committee Has Been Organized 111

With the approval of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, the Ningbo Industrial Bank is instructed to negotiate with Minister Kong to resume business, and the future has a glimmer of hope. Yuan Duanfu, Chen Cuifu, Cao Guohua, Wu Zhihao, Yu Guozhen, Yang Songren, Guo Xuxu, Lin Kanghou, He Shaoyu, He Luting, Wang Beiping, Chen Zhonggao, Zhang Zilian, Wang Honglai, Xiang Shengwu, Wang Boyuan, and others have organized a resumption movement and issued a declaration. The original text of the declaration is recorded as follows: "The Ningbo Industrial Bank is one of the undertakings of our Ningbo people. Since its establishment, its purpose has been to support industry, promote domestic goods, and regulate finance. The person in charge, Mr. Wu Zhihao, is a leader among the leaders of our Ningbo people's undertakings. The suspension of the Ningbo Bank's receipt and remittance is not the same as speculation failures and embezzlement. Therefore, we feel sorry for the stranding of the bank, and thus the resumption movement is launched. There are three reasons for launching the movement: to maintain the interests of creditors, to maintain the reputation of our Ningbo people's undertakings, and to sympathize with Mr. Wu's efforts to save the country with domestic goods. Based on these three points, we will further study the feasibility of its resumption. There are three reasons that show us the possibility of resumption: (1) It is not difficult to resume the bank's business. The debt is only 710,000 yuan. If it can be resumed, the total assets and liabilities are 1.3 million yuan. Excluding the previous capital of 500,000 yuan, collecting accounts at half price can obtain 650,000 yuan, with a difference of 60,000 yuan owed to others. (2) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek will telegraph Minister Kong for relief and resumption of business on record. We think our fellow leaders should support the chairman's wishes and jointly participate in the resumption of business to save the country and the people. (3) The bank's creditors are mostly Ningbo merchants and officials, who have emotional feelings for the resumption of business. The bank has been suspended for more than a month, and the creditors' attitude has been unanimously sympathetic to the resumption of business. The heart of protecting hometown friendship is beyond our expectations. These three points have aroused our enthusiasm for the bank's resumption movement. Therefore, we gather like-minded people to form a sports association, with the bank's directors and supervisors as the main body, and leaders from all walks of life and creditors as guests. The host takes on the responsibilities that should be borne to lay the foundation for resumption, and the guests do their best to help and achieve a common goal. The gathering of Ningbo people's undertakings, the Ningbo Industrial Bank, the base camp for promoting domestic goods, the revival is in sight, and the left coupon can be held. Responsible directors and supervisors, enthusiastic creditors, and leaders from all walks of life who are eager for justice, if you do not believe our words, please join quickly. This announcement." And attached instructions on participating in the subscription: (1) All shareholders, supervisors, and directors of the bank: (A) For shareholders, in order to protect their previous capital, subscribe for new shares to protect their previous benefits. (B) For directors and supervisors, admit to maintaining the resumption of business and unloading responsibilities to protect their reputation. (2) Ningbo leaders and fellow villagers, in order to maintain the reputation of our Ningbo people's undertakings, subscribe for shares to help achieve resumption and complete the glory. (3) The bank's creditors, in order to protect themselves, subscribe for shares to help achieve its resumption, and all deposits are used as cash investment to avoid losses and facilitate the resumption. Regarding the above three points, the association has prepared a share subscription form to solicit subscriptions from all parties. After that, a meeting of subscribers will be convened to discuss it. If there is success, a resumption committee will be organized to carry out the resumption. If there is no considerable success and there is no possibility of resumption, the subscribed shares will be invalid. The association temporarily set up a preparatory office in the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association on Tibet Road. Initiators: Yuan Duanfu, Chen Cuifu, Cao Guohua, Wu Zhihao, Yu Guozhen, Yang Songren, Guo Xuxu, He Shaoyu, He Luting, Wang Beiping, Chen Zhonggao, Zhang Zilian, Lin Kanghou, Wang Honglai, Xiang Shengwu, Wang Boyuan, (Wang and Xiang joined in the capacity of fellow villagers), Zhou Yongsheng, jointly announced.

Shanghai Zhejiang Local Bank Opens 112

The Shanghai branch of Zhejiang Local Bank officially opens today, handling various banking businesses such as deposits, loans, remittances, drafts, and savings. The address of the branch is 381 Jiangxi Road. The manager is Fang Jiyong, and the assistant manager is Jin Boming. The head office is located in Hangzhou, with Zhu Kongyang as the chairman of the board. The directors are Wu Jiao, Ma Yinchu, Ye Yu, Chen Xing, Jin Baishun, etc. The general manager is Xu Enpei, and the deputy general manager is Tang Guanyuan. It is known that the bank was founded in the late Guangxu period of the former Qing Dynasty and has a long history and an outstanding reputation. It was originally called Zhejiang Bank and was entirely government-owned. Later, commercial shares were added, and it was renamed Zhejiang Local Industrial Bank. In 1925, the commercial shares were removed again, and it was renamed its current name. The current paid-up capital is 3 million yuan, and it is approved to have the right to issue banknotes. A total of over 3 million yuan of one-yuan, five-yuan, and ten-yuan notes have been issued, as well as over 400,000 yuan of one-jiao and two-jiao subsidiary currency notes. In recent years, due to the development of its business, branches and offices have been established in important cities. It is reported that there are currently eight established branches and three offices. In addition, there are ten more that are being planned and will be established one after another in the near future.

Refugee and Demobilized Soldiers Shelter - Construction Funds Approved by the Municipal Government - Further Fundraising from Charities if Insufficient - Construction to Begin After Autumn Cools, Completion in October 113

In recent years, due to frequent disasters and rural bankruptcy, demobilized soldiers and refugees have been displaced in Songhu in increasing numbers. Although charitable organizations have tried to provide shelter, tens of thousands are still turned away, making the situation extremely dire. The Municipal Public Security Bureau, in order to provide a safe haven for these homeless demobilized soldiers and refugees and to improve the appearance of the city, has specially planned to build a large-scale shelter to accommodate as many as possible. The estimated cost is 50,000 yuan, which has been approved by the Municipal Government. The funds will be allocated from the municipal treasury. The location of the shelter has been jointly determined with the Municipal Land Bureau to be near the South Railway Station of the Shanghai Garrison, covering an area of about ten mu. The Municipal Public Security Bureau is now preparing to invite bids for construction. If the funds are insufficient in the future, charitable organizations will be asked to assist. Construction is expected to begin after the autumn cools, with completion scheduled for mid-October of this year.

Measures for Building Residences in Huangshan - A Residence Can Be Built for 1,000 Yuan 118

Huangshan in Anhui Province has beautiful and magnificent scenery, surpassing all others in the world. Since the establishment of the Huangshan Construction Committee, it has been working hard on various construction projects, with a grand scale. The first phase of land leasing has been designated, and the number of lessees is increasing daily, almost overwhelming the committee. Recently, in order to promote public welfare, the committee has formulated measures to encourage investment in the construction of public economic housing. The committee will first allocate land for construction, and after the housing is completed, it will collect rent and registration fees according to regulations. The housing is divided into three types: A, B, and C. Type A occupies 60 square meters and costs 3,000 yuan to build. Type B occupies 30 square meters and costs 2,000 yuan to build. Type C occupies 15 square meters and costs 1,000 yuan to build. It is stipulated that the deadline for applying for investment in construction is the end of this year, and it cannot be taken as an example thereafter. It is also stipulated that investors should mutually elect representatives to form a Construction Management Committee with the committee to design and supervise the construction. The construction measures for the housing are very comprehensive and convenient for investors. It is reported that people from Nanjing, Anhui, and other places are eagerly applying for construction. If people from all walks of life in Shanghai want to invest in construction, they can directly contact the committee's Shanghai office at No. 78 Wanyi Lane, Luban Road, French Concession for consultation. The measures are appended below:

Temporary Measures for Encouraging Investment in the Construction of Huangshan Public Economic Housing

(1) The committee will designate the location of the residential area (first designate the various sub-areas of Taoyuan District and Ziyunji in the first residential area) and invite people to jointly invest in the construction of a number of public economic housing units. The committee and the representatives elected by the investors will jointly form a Construction Management Committee to design, build, and manage the project. The aforementioned Construction Management Committee will be dissolved after the construction is completed and the housing is divided. The committee will be responsible for supervising the receipt and expenditure of funds, the construction project, materials, and other matters of the Construction Management Committee, and investors are allowed to participate in the audit at any time. After the housing is completed, the investors will elect representatives to inspect and accept the project together with the engineers sent by the committee. (2) The committee will specially provide land for construction first, and the registration fees and land rent to be paid will be temporarily allowed to be deferred. After the construction is completed, the housing is divided, and the property rights are determined, the various fees will be paid according to regulations, and a lease license will be issued. (3) The construction of public housing by the committee is divided into three types: A, B, and C. Type A housing occupies 60 square meters and costs 3,000 yuan to build per unit. Type B housing occupies 30 square meters and costs 2,000 yuan to build per unit. Type C housing occupies 15 square meters and costs 1,000 yuan to build per unit. Investors may submit housing plans to the Construction Management Committee based on their own opinions or needs. (4) Investors who wish to build a certain type of housing should declare in advance when paying the funds. After the construction is completed, the corresponding properties will be distributed according to the amount of funds paid. (5) After the housing is divided, a lease license is obtained, and the property rights are determined, the property holder is allowed to sell or lease the property, but must not violate the committee's leasing regulations. (6) These measures are aimed at encouraging and promoting investment in construction and strive for universality. Their validity period is limited to this year (1935), and they cannot be taken as an example thereafter. (7) These measures will be implemented upon the resolution of the standing committee of the committee, and any unfulfilled matters may be proposed for modification at any time.

Order of the Meeting: 1. Opening and playing of music; 2. All stand at attention and pay the highest respects to the party and national flag and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen; 3. Play the party song; 4. The chairman respectfully reads Sun Yat-sen's will; 5. The chairman delivers the opening address; 6. Guest speeches; 7. The chairman delivers the speech of thanks; 8. End of the ceremony and playing of music; 9. Entertainment and recreational activities.

Performing Arts: After the ceremony, the performing arts began. Therefore, although the weather was hot and people were sweating profusely, the guests had no fatigue due to the Rendan they had taken for prevention. By the time the performance ended, it was already dawn.

Shareholders Meeting: In addition, the Sino-French Pharmacy held a shareholders meeting at the Lake Society at 4:00 PM yesterday. 97 shareholders attended, representing 23,411 shares, totaling 11,702 rights. Overseas Chinese Association - Vigorously Fights Against Fare Increase - Provides Four Reasons for Objection and Asks Overseas Chinese Federation for Assistance 123

The Shanghai Overseas Chinese Federation received a declaration from the Xiamen Overseas Chinese Association yesterday, asking for effective assistance in vigorously fighting against the fare increase. The original text says, "Xiamen is a trading port, and there are two aspects that give travelers the worst impression: 1. Boatmen take the opportunity to extort; 2. Ticket sales are manipulated and rare. The extortion of boatmen will be cracked down by the water police. The manipulation of ticket sales causes great pain to overseas Chinese. Although the evaluation committee was organized by various agencies last year, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau issued a crackdown, the crackdown is the crackdown, and the manipulation is the manipulation. If this kind of monopoly is not thoroughly eradicated, the overseas Chinese will suffer unnecessary sacrifices, and the new city will leave a huge stain. Only by working together from top to bottom, uniting internally and externally, removing the undue profits of a few people, pursuing the freedom and welfare of the majority, and expressing pure emotions, can we respond to the call for voice. If you agree, you will definitely help a lot. The points that should be fought for are listed below. Please be aware of them. (1) The global recession has spread throughout the islands of Southeast Asia. Our beloved overseas Chinese compatriots have already been forced to return to China. After arriving in their hometowns, they have suffered from the ravages of bandits and communists, and have therefore changed their properties and mortgaged their children to collect travel expenses and return to their countries in droves. The miserable situation is already heart-wrenching to speak of. However, upon arriving in the city, living expenses are not small, and buying tickets is full of twists and turns. After months of accumulation, some have exhausted their funds and returned to their hometowns crying, and some have taken out high-interest loans and made a desperate bet. All kinds of tragedies are not enough. In the eyes of the contractors, it is like robbing on the road, and in the eyes of the overseas Chinese, it is like being kidnapped in broad daylight. (It is found that the fare for each person stipulated by various shipping companies is 61 yuan, but when the contractors sell it, they charge from 120 yuan to 150 or 60 yuan.) The number of people exported from this port every year is estimated to be no less than tens of thousands. These tens of thousands of people groan under the extortion of ticket merchants, and the money wasted is a shocking number. The flow of people on the road, who will describe it? In terms of the suffering of overseas Chinese, this is the first thing that should be fought for. (2) People in the mainland cannot go abroad, so they must still return to their hometowns. When they return to their hometowns, their industries are exhausted, and they do not have the means to live, and they are hungry and cold. The father may not have his son, and how can the officials have their people? Therefore, it is not easy to eliminate bandits and communists in southern Fujian. Although it is related to the economic collapse and rural bankruptcy, there are also other reasons. However, those who are forced to go astray due to high fares and lack of progress account for at least a certain proportion. If this continues without thinking of reform, not only will the Sun Yat-sen's Principle of People's Livelihood be completely destroyed, but also the security of this port and the mainland will be in danger. In terms of local pacification, this is the second thing that should be fought for. (3) Overseas Chinese are the mother of the revolution, Sun Yat-sen often said. Therefore, the central authorities and local governments have been protecting overseas Chinese for a long time. However, when we look at the overseas Chinese living in various places, they are oppressed and expelled, and we hear about it every day. This is still a matter of national rights, and we are exhausted. Everyone understands it. If Xiamen is clearly a place where authority can reach, and ticket merchants are also people who can be controlled by government orders, if even this most common and shocking accumulation of poison cannot be eliminated, then there is not enough protection abroad, and this generation is allowed to bully at will in China. The inward-looking heart is discouraged, and the road to making a living is cut off. This association has no face to thank. What will the authorities say to explain themselves? In terms of government orders, this is the third thing that should be fought for. (4) It is found that the fare for going abroad in the past was only 10 yuan, and at most it reached more than 20 yuan. Since the issue of import restrictions, shipping companies took the opportunity to manipulate and uniformly set the price at 61 yuan, which has increased by two or three times compared to the past. If there were no contractors to fuel the flames, this pricing would be difficult to sustain. Now, the contractors are charging so much outside of the 61 yuan. Various companies are fortunate enough that the tickets are profitable and will not increase the price again. It is impossible to reduce them. It only increases the burden on overseas Chinese and increases the income of foreigners. What is the difference between harming the group and flattering foreigners? In terms of recovering rights, this is the fourth thing that should be fought for. In short, this association is organized by overseas Chinese in Fujian Province, and it speaks for overseas Chinese and does not ask about other things. We only ask that the contractors in the city do not hoard and sell tickets, and that overseas Chinese who go abroad can buy tickets freely. The goal is achieved, and we are satisfied. That's all. On the 13th of last month, it was the date of the executive committee meeting of this association. Due to public discussions and resolutions, we will report to the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission on the method of treating both the symptoms and the root causes, and shout loudly to fulfill our duties. However, although this case should be fought for, our colleagues have no strength. Therefore, we disclose the situation and hope that the government authorities and various legal entities will support justice and provide effective assistance. We hereby declare solemnly and hope that everyone will understand."
